 mahabhiyog prastaav tab laayaa jaataa he jab aisa lage ki in padon par baithe log samvidhan kaa ullaghann yaa durvyavhaar kar rahe hon
 If this is happening, then the proposal of grand appointment can be brought in any House
 iskaa zikr samvidhan ke anuchhed 62, 124 (4), (5), 217 or 218 main kiya gaya he
 Impeachment process The process of impeachment motion is considered to be extremely complex
 loksabhaa main is prastaav ko laane ke liye 100 saansadon ke hastakshar chahie
 At the same time, signatures of 50 mps are required to bring it in Rajya Sabha
 agar ye sadan main pesh hota he to sadan ke adhyaksh is par faisla lenge
 If they want, they can accept it or they can also reject it
 agar adhyaksh mahabhiyog prastaav ko sweekaar kar lete hai to teen sadasyon kii ek cameti aaropon kii jaanch karegi
 This committee consists of a judge of the Supreme Court, a Chief Justice of the High Court and one other person
 agarjaanch cametico aarope sahi lagate hai to hi mahabhiyog prastaav par sansad main bahes hogi
 After this, the motion needs to be passed by a two-thirds majority in both houses of Parliament
 agar donon sadan main ye prastaav paarit ho jaataa he to ise manzuri ke liye raashtrapati ke paas bheja jayega
 Explain that only the President has the right to remove any judge

 Now on September 20, just before the mains examination will be held, the UPSC has issued the necessary guidelines for the candidates
 civil seva pariksha (CSE) ke duusare charan main ummidavaaron ko bahut dhyaan rakhana hoga
 a little mistake can break your dream
 aapkaa upiessi ke jariye bhartiya prashasnic seva (IAS), bhartiya videsh seva (IFS), bhartiya police seva (IPS) or bhartiya rajasav sevaaon (IRS) main sevaayen dene kaa mauka bhi chhot saktaa he
 List of Do's and Don't's released UPSC has prepared a PDF of 21 pages to tell Do's and Don't's
 is peedief main chitron or udaahranon ke jariye puri baat samajhaaii gai he
 This PDF has been released on the official website of UPSC
 ye peedief dhyaan se padhein, isse aapako pataa chalegaa ki kis tarah aap mens likhte vakt choti-choti galatiyon se bachakar behatar rigelt paa sakate hai
 Do not write Om or 786, there will be mistake
 Candidates appearing in the UPSC exam often make the mistake that they write an auspicious number or mantra on their question-less answer booklet (QCAB)
 ummidavaar apni dharmik manyata ke lihaaj se kabhi cross kaa chinh to kabhi uun yaa 786 likh dete hai
 Here UPSC has clearly stated that on QCAB write only the answers related to the answer
 bina vajah kii baaten yahaan na likhe, isse ejaminner par bura asar padataa he
 Do not open the identity The answer sheet of the candidate is identified by the serial number and roll number
 aisa bhi dekha gaya he ki kuch ummidavaar apni bocolate par apana naam yaa paariwarik sthiti vagairah likh dete hai
 Such candidates may find this mistake overwhelming
 upiessi ne kaha he ki QCAB main aisa kuch naa likhen, jisase unki pahchaan jaahir ho
 In this, you cannot give name, roll number and signature
 ye bhi dhyaan rakhenummidavaaron se ye bhi kaha gaya he ki wo bhashaaen badalakar uttar na den
 Use only one language to answer
 iske alaava agar aap kuch uttar pen se or kuch pencil se likhte hai to ye bhi galat he
 No emotional atrocities will work
 Candidates have also been instructed not to attempt any 'emotional atrocities' on the examiner
 iskaa sidhaa matlab he ki ummidavaar apni copy par koi dastaan likhakar apil nahin kar saktaa he
 Apart from this, care should also be taken on writing, it should be clear for the examiner
